Source Code

These source-code files were from the printout at the MIT Museum, with many thanks to Deborah Douglas, the Museum's Curator of Science and Technology, for releasing it to us. The printout was digitally photographed by Paul Fjeld. A team of volunteers transcribed the source code manually from these images or, where appropriate, modified already-transcribed but similar source Luminary 131 (Apollo 13) source code to agree with the images from the printout. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that higher-quality images are available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 001 OF AGC PROGRAM LMY99 BY NASA 2021112-061
	20'35 OCT. 28,1968
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision.

Note: Notations below resembling this note are 21st-century annotations added by the Virtual AGC project, and are not original AGC source code. 

016450,000033:                                                                                                  #  Page 390
016451,000034:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME -- KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016452,000035:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO -- 4           DATE -- 27 APRIL 1967           ASSEMBLY -- PINDANCE REV 18
016453,000036:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY -- FILENE
016454,000037:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION -- PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
016455,000038: 
016456,000039:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
016457,000040: 
016458,000041:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
016459,000042:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
016460,000043:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
016461,000044:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAM, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
016462,000045: 
016463,000046:                                                                                                  #  THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
016464,000047:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
016465,000048:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
016466,000049:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
016467,000050:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
016468,000051: 
016469,000052:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
016470,000053:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS (THESE
016471,000054:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
016472,000055:                                                                                                  #  'EXTENDED VERBS').
016473,000056: 
016474,000057:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION 'ASSEMBLY AND 
016475,000058:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION'.
016476,000059:

Ramón Alonso, one of the original AGC developers, provides a little more insight: Apparently, nobody had yet arrived at any kind of software requirements for the AGC's user interface when the desire arose within the Instrumentation Laboratory to set up a demo guidance-computer unit with which to impress visitors to the lab. Of course, this demo would have to do something, if it was going to be at all impressive, and to do something it would need some software. In short order, some of the coders threw together a demo program, inventing and using the verb/noun user-interface concept (in the whimsical fashion seen in much of this code), but without any idea that the verb/noun concept would somehow survive into the flight software. As time passed, and more and more people became familiar with the demo, nobody got around to inventing an improvement for the user interface, so the coders simply built it into the flight software without any specific requirements to do so.

However, that does not mean that the verb/noun interface was universally beloved. Ramón says that many objections were received from naysayers, such as "it's not scientific", "it's not dignified", or even "astronauts won't understand it". Even though the coders of the demo hadn't seriously intended the verb/noun interface to be used in any permanent way, it became a kind of devilish game to counter these objections with (perhaps) sophistic arguments as to why the interface was really a good one. In the end, the coders won. I don't know whether they were elated or dismayed by this victory.

The astronauts, of course, could understand the interface, but they did not like it. Most of them really wanted an interface much more like that they had used in aircraft: i.e., lots of dials and switches. Dave Scott is the the only astronaut I'm aware of who had kind words for it (or for the AGC in general), though we are told that Jim McDivitt wasn't necessary completely hostile to it.

—Ron Burkey, 07/2009

016511,000094: 
016512,000095:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES --
016513,000096: 
016514,000097:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
016515,000098:                                                                                                  #  EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES AN INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
016516,000099:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
016517,000100:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
016518,000101:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT 'CHARIN'), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016519,000102: 
016520,000103:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
016521,000104:                                                                                                  #  EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT, WHICH
016522,000105:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
016523,000106:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT 'CHARIN') AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016524,000107: 
016525,000108:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
016526,000109:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT `NVSUB' WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
016527,000110:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
016528,000111:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE 'NVSUB' AND 'NVSBWAIT' (SEE
016529,000112:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016530,000113: 
016531,000114:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES --
016532,000115: 
016533,000116:                                                                                                  #        IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
016534,000117:                                                                                                  #                1)      ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
016535,000118:                                                                                                  #                2)      EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE
016536,000119:                                                                                                  #  Page 391
016537,000120:                                                                                                  #                        PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
016538,000121:                                                                                                  #                        RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTEDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
016539,000122:                                                                                                  #                        CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
016540,000123:                                                                                                  #                        ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB.  EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
016541,000124:                                                                                                  #                3)      VERB 37.  CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS 'V37' IN THE
016542,000125:                                                                                                  #                        SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
016543,000126:                                                                                                  #                        30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
016544,000127:                                                                                                  #                4)      KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS 'PINBRNCH' IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
016545,000128:                                                                                                  #                        ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
016546,000129:                                                                                                  #                        THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND 'CADRSTOR' IS NOT +0.
016547,000130: 
016548,000131:                                                                                                  #  IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
016549,000132:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
016550,000133:                                                                                                  #  'NVSUB' AND 'NVSBWAIT' (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016551,000134: 
016552,000135:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES --
016553,000136: 
016554,000137:                                                                                                  #        EXTERNAL INITIATION:
016555,000138:                                                                                                  #        IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
016556,000139:                                                                                                  #        ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO 'ENDOFJOB'.
016557,000140: 
016558,000141:                                                                                                  #        INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
016559,000142:                                                                                                  #        IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
016560,000143:                                                                                                  #        (WITH OCTAL 01501).
016561,000144:                                                                                                  #        IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
016562,000145:                                                                                                  #        CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
016563,000146:                                                                                                  #                1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
016564,000147:                                                                                                  #                2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
016565,000148: 
016566,000149:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
016567,000150:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016568,000151: 
016569,000152:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT --
016570,000153: 
016571,000154:                                                                                                  #  INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE 'DSPTAB'
016572,000155:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL). 'DSPOUT' (A PART OF T4RUPT)
016573,000156:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE 'DSPTAB' INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
016574,000157:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
016575,000158: 
016576,000159:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION --
016577,000160: 
016578,000161:                                                                                                  #  FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
016579,000162:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN 'STARTSUB'.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
016580,000163:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
016581,000164:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
016582,000165: 
016583,000166:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR
016584,000167:                                                                                                  #  Page 392
016585,000168:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
016586,000169: 
016587,000170:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST --
016588,000171: 
016589,000172:                                                                                                  #  REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
016590,000173:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PACE NUMBERS.
016591,000174: 
016592,000175:                                                                                                  #        NVSUB           CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
016593,000176:                                                                                                  #                        OF RELATED INTEREST     NVSBWAIT
016594,000177:                                                                                                  #                                                NVSUBUSY
016595,000178:                                                                                                  #                                                PRENVBSY
016596,000179: 
016597,000180:                                                                                                  #        ENDIDLE         ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO TO SLEEP WHILE
016598,000181:                                                                                                  #                        AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
016599,000182: 
016600,000183:                                                                                                  #        DSPMM           ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
016601,000184:                                                                                                  #                        PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
016602,000185:                                                                                                  #                        (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
016603,000186:                                                                                                  #                        FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
016604,000187: 
016605,000188:                                                                                                  #        BLANKSUB        ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
016606,000189:                                                                                                  #                        COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
016607,000190: 
016608,000191:                                                                                                  #        JAMTERM         ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
016609,000192:                                                                                                  #        JAMPROC         TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
016610,000193: 
016611,000194:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR         VERBS FOR PERIODIC (1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
016612,000195: 
016613,000196:                                                                                                  #        PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
016614,000197:                                                                                                  #                REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
016615,000198:                                                                                                  #                THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE 'NVSUB' (SEE
016616,000199:                                                                                                  #                SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016617,000200: 
016618,000201:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
016619,000202:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE 'DSPABC' (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016620,000203: 
016621,000204:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION 'PINBALL NOUN
016622,000205:                                                                                                  #        TABLES'.
016623,000206: 
016624,000207:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
016625,000208:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
016626,000209:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016627,000210:

The document described above, "Keyboard and Display Program Operation" by Alan I. Green and Robert J. Filene is available online at the Virtual AGC website. —Ron Burkey, 07/2009

016635,000218: 
016636,000219:                                                                                                  #  "IT WILL BE PROVED TO THY FACE THAT THOU HAST MEN ABOUT THEE THAT
016637,000220:                                                                                                  #  USUALLY TALK OF A NOUN AND A VERB, AND SUCH ABOMINABLE WORDS AS NO
016638,000221:                                                                                                  #  Page 393
016639,000222:                                                                                                  #  CHRISTIAN EAR CAN ENDURE TO HEAR."
016640,000223:                                                                                                  #                                        HENRY 6, ACT 2, SCENE 4
016641,000224:

Actually, this quotation is from Henry VI, Part 2, Act IV, Scene VII. —Ron Burkey, 07/2009 

016644,000227: 
016645,000228:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
016646,000229: 
016647,000230:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT      ERASE                   # DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
016648,000231:                                                                                                  #  DECBRNCH      ERASE                   # +DEC, -DEC, OCT INDICATOR
016649,000232:                                                                                                  #  VERBREG       ERASE                   # VERB CODE
016650,000233:                                                                                                  #  NOUNREG       ERASE                   # NOUN CODE
016651,000234:                                                                                                  #  XREG          ERASE                   # R1 INPUT BUFFER
016652,000235:                                                                                                  #  YREG          ERASE                   # R2 INPUT BUFFER
016653,000236:                                                                                                  #  ZREG          ERASE                   # R3 INPUT BUFFER
016654,000237:                                                                                                  #  XREGLP        ERASE                   # LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016655,000238:                                                                                                  #  YREGLP        ERASE                   # LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016656,000239:                                                                                                  #  HITEMOUT      =       YREGLP          # TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016657,000240:                                                                                                  #                                        #       MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
016658,000241:                                                                                                  #  ZREGLP        ERASE                   # LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016659,000242:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMOUT      =       ZREGLP          # TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016660,000243:                                                                                                  #                                        #       MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
016661,000244:                                                                                                  #  MODREG        ERASE                   # MODE CODE
016662,000245:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK       ERASE                   # KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
016663,000246:                                                                                                  #  REQRET        ERASE                   # RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
016664,000247:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      ERASE                   # STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
016665,000248:                                                                                                  #  CLPASS        ERASE                   # PASS INDICATOR FOR CLEAR
016666,000249:                                                                                                  #  NOUT          ERASE                   # ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
016667,000250:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR      ERASE                   # MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
016668,000251:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE       ERASE                   # N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
016669,000252:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1      ERASE                   # NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR (MATBS) = MONSAVE+1
016670,000253:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE2      ERASE                   # NVMONOPT OPTIONS
016671,000254:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB        ERASE           +13D    # 0-10, DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER, 11-13, C RELAYS
016672,000255:                                                                                                  #  CADRSTOR      ERASE                   # ENDIDLE STORAGE
016673,000256:                                                                                                  #  NVQTEM        ERASE                   # NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
016674,000257:                                                                                                  #                                        # MUST = NVBNKTEM-1.
016675,000258:                                                                                                  #  NVBNKTEM      ERASE                   # NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
016676,000259:                                                                                                  #                                        # MUST = NVQTEM+1
016677,000260:                                                                                                  #  VERBSAVE      ERASE                   # NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
016678,000261:                                                                                                  #  DSPLIST       ERASE                   # WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
016679,000262:                                                                                                  #  EXTVBACT      ERASE                   # EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
016680,000263:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM1       ERASE                   # BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
016681,000264:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM2       ERASE                   # BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
016682,000265: 
016683,000266:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016684,000267: 
016685,000268:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016686,000269: 
016687,000270:                                                                                                  #  Page 394
016688,000271: 
016689,000272:                                                                                                  #  DSEXIT        =       INTB15+         # RETURN FOR DSPIN
016690,000273:                                                                                                  #  EXITEM        =       INTB15+         # RETURN FOR SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE SELECT
016691,000274:                                                                                                  #  BLANKRET      =       INTB15+         # RETURN FOR 2BLANK
016692,000275: 
016693,000276:                                                                                                  #  WRDRET        =       INTBIT15        # RETURN FOR 5BLANK.
016694,000277:                                                                                                  #  WDRET         =       INTBIT15        # RETURN FOR DSPWD
016695,000278:                                                                                                  #  DECRET        =       INTBIT15        # RETURN FOR PUTCOM(DEC LOAD)
016696,000279:                                                                                                  #  21/22REG      =       INTBIT15        # TEMP FOR CHARIN
016697,000280: 
016698,000281:                                                                                                  #  UPDATRET      =       POLISH          # RETURN FOR UPDATNN, UPDATVB
016699,000282:                                                                                                  #  CHAR          =       POLISH          # TEMP FOR CHARIN
016700,000283:                                                                                                  #  ERCNT         =       POLISH          # COUNTER FOR ERROR LIGHT RESET
016701,000284:                                                                                                  #  DECOUNT       =       POLISH          # COUNTER FOR SCALING AND DISPLAY (DEC)
016702,000285: 
016703,000286:                                                                                                  #  SGNON         =       VBUF            # TEMP FOR +,- ON
016704,000287:                                                                                                  #  NOUNTEM       =       VBUF            # COUNTER FOR MIXNOUN FETCH
016705,000288:                                                                                                  #  DISTEM        =       VBUF            # COUNTER FOR OCTAL DISPLAY VERB
016706,000289:                                                                                                  #  DECTEM        =       VBUF            # COUNTER FOR FETCH (DEC DISPLAY VERBS)
016707,000290: 
016708,000291:                                                                                                  #  SGNOFF        =       VBUF    +1      # TEMP FOR +,- ON
016709,000292:                                                                                                  #  NVTEMP        =       VBUF    +1      # TEMP FOR NVSUB
016710,000293:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP1       =       VBUF    +1      # STORAGE FOR SF CONST HI PART (=SFTEMP2-1)
016711,000294:                                                                                                  #  HITEMIN       =       VBUF    +1      # TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016712,000295:                                                                                                  #                                        #       MUST = LOTEMIN-1.
016713,000296:                                                                                                  #  CODE          =       VBUF    +2      # FOR DSPIN
016714,000297:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP2       =       VBUF    +2      # STORAGE FOR SF CONST LO PART (=SFTEMP1+1)
016715,000298:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMIN       =       VBUF    +2      # TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016716,000299:                                                                                                  #                                        #       MUST = HITEMIN+1
016717,000300:                                                                                                  #  MIXTEMP       =       VBUF    +3      # FOR MIXNOUN DATA
016718,000301:                                                                                                  #  SIGNRET       =       VBUF    +3      # RETURN FOR +,- ON
016719,000302:                                                                                                  #  ALSO MIXTEMP+1 = VBUF+4, MIXTEMP+2 = VBUF+5.
016720,000303: 
016721,000304:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET        =       DOTINC          # EXIT FROM ENTER
016722,000305: 
016723,000306:                                                                                                  #  WDCNT         =       DOTRET          # CHAR COUNTER FOR DSPWD
016724,000307:                                                                                                  #  INREL         =       DOTRET          # INPUT BUFFER SELECTOR (X, Y, Z, REG)
016725,000308: 
016726,000309:                                                                                                  #  DSPMMTEM      =       MATINC          # DSPCOUNT SAVE FOR DSPMM
016727,000310:                                                                                                  #  MIXBR         =       MATINC          # INDICATOR FOR MIXED OR NORMAL NOUN
016728,000311: 
016729,000312:                                                                                                  #  TEM1          ERASE                   # EXEC TEMP
016730,000313:                                                                                                  #  DSREL         =       TEM1            # REL ADDRESS FOR DSPIN
016731,000314: 
016732,000315:                                                                                                  #  TEM2          ERASE                   # EXEC TEMP
016733,000316:                                                                                                  #  DSMAG         =       TEM2            # MAGNITUDE STORE FOR DSPIN
016734,000317:                                                                                                  #  IDADDTEM      =       TEM2            # MIXNOUN INDIRECT ADDRESS STORAGE
016735,000318:                                                                                                  #  TEM3          ERASE                   # EXEC TEMP
016736,000319:                                                                                                  #  COUNT         =       TEM3            # FOR DSPIN
016737,000320: 
016738,000321:                                                                                                  #  Page 395
016739,000322:                                                                                                  #  TEM4          ERASE                   # EXEC TEMP
016740,000323:                                                                                                  #  LSTPTR        =       TEM4            # LIST POINTER FOR GRABUSY
016741,000324:                                                                                                  #  RELRET        =       TEM4            # RETURN FOR RELDSP
016742,000325:                                                                                                  #  FREERET       =       TEM4            # RETURN FOR FREEDSP
016743,000326:                                                                                                  #  DSPWDRET      =       TEM4            # RETURN FOR DSPSIGN
016744,000327:                                                                                                  #  SEPSCRET      =       TEM4            # RETURN FOR SEPSEC
016745,000328:                                                                                                  #  SEPMNRET      =       TEM4            # RETURN FOR SEPMIN
016746,000329: 
016747,000330:                                                                                                  #  TEM5          ERASE                   # EXEC TEMP
016748,000331:                                                                                                  #  NOUNADD       =       TEM5            # TEMP STORAGE FOR NOUN ADDRESS
016749,000332: 
016750,000333:                                                                                                  #  NNADTEM       ERASE                   # TEMP FOR NOUN ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY
016751,000334:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTEM      ERASE                   # TEMP FOR NOUN TYPE TABLE ENTRY
016752,000335:                                                                                                  #  IDAD1TEM      ERASE                   # TEMP FOR INDIR ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016753,000336:                                                                                                  #                                        # MUST = IDAD2TEM-1, = IDAD3TEM-2.
016754,000337:                                                                                                  #  IDAD2TEM      ERASE                   # TEMP FOR INDIR ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016755,000338:                                                                                                  #                                        # MUST = IDAD1TEM+1, IDAD3TEM-1.
016756,000339:                                                                                                  #  IDAD3TEM      ERASE                   # TEMP FOR INDIR ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016757,000340:                                                                                                  #                                        # MUST = IDAD1TEM+2, IDAD2TEM+1.

016759,000342: 
016760,000343:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION.
016761,000344: 
016762,000345:                                                                                                  #  ADDITIONAL TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016763,000346: 
016764,000347:                                                                                                  #        MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
016765,000348:                                                                                                  #        BUF, +1, +2
016766,000349:                                                                                                  #        BUF2, +1, +2
016767,000350:                                                                                                  #        MPTEMP
016768,000351:                                                                                                  #        ADDRWD
016769,000352:

016771,000354: 
016772,000355:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016773,000356:

016775,000358:                                                                                                  #  UPLOCK        ERASE                   # BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
016776,000359:                                                                                                  #                                        # RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)
016777,000360: 
016778,000361:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION

016780,000363:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016781,000364: 
016782,000365:                                                                                                  #  KEYTEMP1      =       WAITEXIT        # TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
016783,000366:                                                                                                  #  DSRUPTEM      =       WAITEXIT        # TEMP FOR DSPOUT

016785,000368:

016787,000370: 
016788,000371:                                                                                                  #  Page 396
016789,000372:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
016790,000373:                                                                                                  #  0             10000
016791,000374:                                                                                                  #  1             00001
016792,000375:                                                                                                  #  9             01001
016793,000376:                                                                                                  #  VERB          10001
016794,000377:                                                                                                  #  ERROR RES     10010
016795,000378:                                                                                                  #  KEY RLSE      11001
016796,000379:                                                                                                  #  +             11010
016797,000380:                                                                                                  #  -             11011
016798,000381:                                                                                                  #  ENTER         11100
016799,000382:                                                                                                  #  CLEAR         11110
016800,000383:                                                                                                  #  NOUN          11111
016801,000384: 
016802,000385:                                                                                                  #  (2003 RSB -- The PROCEED key has no keycode; it is read by an alternate mechanism.)
016803,000386: 
016804,000387:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL.  SET OUT0 TO AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
016805,000388:                                                                                                  #  A'S   SELECTS A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
016806,000389:                                                                                                  #        ENERGIZED.
016807,000390:                                                                                                  #  B     FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
016808,000391:                                                                                                  #  C'S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
016809,000392:                                                                                                  #  D'S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
016810,000393: 
016811,000394:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
016812,000395:                                                                                                  #  MD1   MD2                             (MAJOR MODE)
016813,000396:                                                                                                  #  VD1   VD2 (VERB)      ND1     ND2     (NOUN)
016814,000397:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  R1D2    R1D3    R1D4    R1D5    (R1)
016815,000398:                                                                                                  #  R2D1  R2D2    R2D3    R2D4    R2D5    (R2)
016816,000399:                                                                                                  #  R3D1  R3D2    R3D3    R3D4    R3D5    (R3)
016817,000400: 
016818,000401:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
016819,000402: 
016820,000403:                                                                                                  #  MD1   25              R2D1    11              ALL ARE OCTAL
016821,000404:                                                                                                  #  MD2   24              R2D2    10
016822,000405:                                                                                                  #  VD1   23              R2D3     7
016823,000406:                                                                                                  #  VD2   22              R2D4     6
016824,000407:                                                                                                  #  ND1   21              R2D5     5
016825,000408:                                                                                                  #  ND2   20              R3D1     4
016826,000409:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  16              R3D2     3
016827,000410:                                                                                                  #  R1D2  15              R3D3     2
016828,000411:                                                                                                  #  R1D3  14              R3D4     1
016829,000412:                                                                                                  #  R1D4  13              R3D5     0
016830,000413:                                                                                                  #  R1D5  12
016831,000414: 
016832,000415:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11-REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
016833,000416: 
016834,000417:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB                RELAYWD         BIT11           BITS 10-6       BITS 5-1
016835,000418:                                                                                                  #  RELADD
016836,000419:                                                                                                  #  10            1011                            MD1 (25)        MD2 (24)
016837,000420:                                                                                                  #  9             1010                            VD1 (23)        VD2 (22)
016838,000421:                                                                                                  #  8             1001                            ND1 (21)        ND2 (20)
016839,000422:                                                                                                  #  7             1000                                            R1D1 (16)
016840,000423:                                                                                                  #  Page 397
016841,000424:                                                                                                  #  6             0111            +R1             R1D2 (15)       R1D3 (14)
016842,000425:                                                                                                  #  5             0110            -R1             R1D4 (13)       R1D5 (12)
016843,000426:                                                                                                  #  4             0101            +R2             R2D1 (11)       R2D2 (10)
016844,000427:                                                                                                  #  3             0100            -R2             R2D3 (7)        R2D4 (6)
016845,000428:                                                                                                  #  2             0011                            R2D5 (5)        R3D1 (4)
016846,000429:                                                                                                  #  1             0010            +R3             R3D2 (3)        R3D3 (2)
016847,000430:                                                                                                  #  0             0001            -R3             R3D4 (1)        R3D5 (0)
016848,000431:                                                                                                  #                0000        NO RELAYWORD
016849,000432: 
016850,000433:                                                                                                  #  THE 5-BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
016851,000434: 
016852,000435:                                                                                                  #  BLANK 00000
016853,000436:                                                                                                  #  0     10101
016854,000437:                                                                                                  #  1     00011
016855,000438:                                                                                                  #  2     11001
016856,000439:                                                                                                  #  3     11011
016857,000440:                                                                                                  #  4     01111
016858,000441:                                                                                                  #  5     11110
016859,000442:                                                                                                  #  6     11100
016860,000443:                                                                                                  #  7     10011
016861,000444:                                                                                                  #  8     11101
016862,000445:                                                                                                  #  9     11111
016863,000446: 
016864,000447:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
016865,000448: 
016866,000449:                                                                                                  #        KEY RELEASE LIGHT       -       BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
016867,000450:                                                                                                  #        VERB/NOUN FLASH         -       BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
016868,000451:                                                                                                  #        OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT    -       BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11
016869,000452:

017550,001133: 41,2344           31001                           CA       VERBREG                               
017551,001134: 41,2345           04635        UPDAT1             TC       POSTJUMP                              #  CANT USE SWCALL TO GO TO DSPDECVN, SINCE
017552,001135: 41,2346           61317                           CADR     GOVNUPDT                              #  UPDATVB CAN ITSELF BE CALLED BY SWCALL.
017553,001136: 41,2347           00117                           TC       UPDATRET                              
017554,001137: 
017555,001138: 41,2350           04145        GOALMCYC           TC       ALMCYCLE                              #  NEEDED BECAUSE BANKJUMP CANT HANDLE F/F.
017556,001139: 
017557,001140: 41,2351           04635        GODSPALM           TC       POSTJUMP                              
017558,001141: 41,2352           61420                           CADR     DSPALARM                              
017559,001142: 
017560,001143:                                                                                                  #  Page 413
017561,001144:                                                                                                  #  NOUN TABLES
017562,001145: 
017563,001146:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
017564,001147:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
017565,001148:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR (E OR F) TO
017566,001149:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED.  -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
017567,001150:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
017568,001151: 
017569,001152:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS (IDADDREL) IN LOW
017570,001153:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
017571,001154: 
017572,001155:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
017573,001156: 
017574,001157:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE,  M'S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
017575,001158:                                                                                                  #                        N'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
017576,001159:                                                                                                  #                        P'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
017577,001160: 
017578,001161:                                                                                                  #  MIXED-CASE,           M'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER    3 COMPONENT CASE
017579,001162:                                                                                                  #                        N'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
017580,001163:                                                                                                  #                        P'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017581,001164:                                                                                                  #                        N'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER    2 COMPONENT CASE
017582,001165:                                                                                                  #                        P'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017583,001166:                                                                                                  #                        P'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER    1 COMPONENT CASE
017584,001167: 
017585,001168:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE (IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
017586,001169:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
017587,001170:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
017588,001171: 
017589,001172:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE (RUTMXTAB) FOR MIXED
017590,001173:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY.  THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN.  THE FORM IS,
017591,001174: 
017592,001175:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
017593,001176: 
017594,001177:                                                                                                  #  Q'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER          3 COMPONENT CASE
017595,001178:                                                                                                  #  R'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
017596,001179:                                                                                                  #  S'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017597,001180:                                                                                                  #  R'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER          2 COMPONENT CASE
017598,001181:                                                                                                  #  S'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017599,001182: 
017600,001183:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
017601,001184:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
017602,001185:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
017603,001186: 
017604,001187:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
017605,001188:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
017606,001189:

017916,001499:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ROUTINE DISPLAYS TWO CONTIGUOUS SP POSITIVE INTEGERS
017917,001500:                                                                                                  #  AS TWO POSITIVE DECIMAL INTEGERS IN RXD1-RXD2 AND RXD4-RXD5 (RXD3 IS
017918,001501:                                                                                                  #  BLANKED).  THE INTEGER IN THE LOWER NUMBERED ADDRESS IS DISPLAYED IN
017919,001502:                                                                                                  #  RXD1-RXD2.
017920,001503:

017922,001505: 40,2733           02413                           TC       +ON                                   #  TURN ON + SIGN

017925,001508: 40,2736           46245                           CS       THREE                                 
017926,001509: 40,2737           50117                           INDEX    DECOUNT                               
017927,001510: 40,2740           64317                           AD       R1D1                                  #  RXD4
017928,001511: 40,2741           54777                           TS       DSPCOUNT

017930,001513: 40,2743           30155                           CA       MPAC       +1                         
017931,001514: 40,2744           03306                           TC       DSPDECVN                              #  DISPLAY 2ND INTEGER (LIKE VERB AND NOUN)
017932,001515: 40,2745           04635                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
017933,001516: 40,2746           62570                           CADR     DSPDCEND   +2                         
017934,001517: 
017935,001518:                                                                                                  #  READLO PICKS UP FRESHDATA FOR BOTH HI AND LO AND LEAVES IT IN 
017936,001519:                                                                                                  #  MPAC, MPAC+1.  THIS IS NEEDED FOR TIME DISPLAY.  IT ZEROES MPAC+2, BUT
017937,001520:                                                                                                  #  DOES NOT FORCE TPAGREE.

018123,001706: 
018124,001707:                                                                                                  #  THIS IS A SPECIAL PURPOS VERB FOR DISPLAYING A DOUBLE PRECISION AGC
018125,001708:                                                                                                  #  WORD AS 10 DECIMAL DIGITS ON THE AGC DISPLAY PANEL.  IT CAN BE USED WITH
018126,001709:                                                                                                  #  ANY NOUN, EXCEPT MIXED NOUNS. IT DISPLAYS THE CONTENTS
018127,001710:                                                                                                  #  OF THE REGISTER NOUNADD IS POINTING TO.  IF USED WITH NOUNS WHICH ARE
018128,001711:                                                                                                  #  INHERENTLY NOT DP SUCH AS THE CDU COUNTERS THE DISPLAY WILL BE GARBAGE.
018129,001712:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY IS IN R1 AND R2 ONLY WITH THE SIGN IN R1.
018130,001713: 
018131,001714: 40,2771                                           SETLOC   ENDRDLO    +1

018137,001720: 40,2774           03420                           TC       DSPALARM                              
018138,001721: 40,2775           00006                           EXTEND

018140,001723: 40,2777           30001                           DCA      0

018149,001732: 
018150,001733:                                                                                                  #  Page 425
018151,001734:                                                                                                  #  LOAD VERBS            IF ALARM CONDITION IS DETECTED DURING EXECUTE,
018152,001735:                                                                                                  #  CHECK FAIL LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND ENDOFJOB.  IF ALARM CONDITION IS
018153,001736:                                                                                                  #  DETECTED DURING ENTER OF DATA, CHECK FAIL IS TURNED ON AND IT RECYCLES
018154,001737:                                                                                                  #  TO EXECUTE OF ORIGINAL LOAD VERB.  RECYCLE CAUSED BY  1) DECIMAL MACHINE
018155,001738:                                                                                                  #  CADR  2) MIXTURE OF OCTAL/DECIMAL DATA  3) OCTAL DATA INTO DECIMAL
018156,001739:                                                                                                  #  ONLY NOUN  4) DEC DATA INTO OCT ONLY NOUN  5) DATA TOO LARGE FOR SCALE
018157,001740:                                                                                                  #  6) FEWER THAN 3 DATA WORDS LOADED FOR HRS, MIN, SEC NOUN.  (2)-(6) ALARM
018158,001741:                                                                                                  #  AND RECYCLE OCCUR AT FINAL ENTER OF SET. (1) ALARM AND RECYCLE OCCUR AT
018159,001742:                                                                                                  #  ENTER OF CADR.

018713,002296: 42,3601           03603                           TC       FORCEV25                              
018714,002297: 42,3602           00002                           TC       Q                                     
018715,002298: 
018716,002299: 42,3603           46010        FORCEV25           CS       OCT31                                 #  FORCE VERB 25 TO BE EXECUTED BY RECYCLE
018717,002300: 42,3604           55041                           TS       VERBSAVE                              #  IN CASE OPERATOR EXECUTED A LOWER LOAD
018718,002301: 42,3605           04145                           TC       ALMCYCLE                              #  VERB.  ALARM AND RECYCLE.
018719,002302: 42,3606                        ENDHMSS            EQUALS                                         
018720,002303: 
018721,002304:                                                                                                  #  Page 437
018722,002305:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
018723,002306:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
018724,002307:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
018725,002308:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
018726,002309:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
018727,002310: 
018728,002311:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
018729,002312:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
018730,002313:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
018731,002314:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
018732,002315:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
018733,002316:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
018734,002317:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
018735,002318: 
018736,002319:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
018737,002320:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018738,002321:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018739,002322: 
018740,002323:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
018741,002324:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
018742,002325: 
018743,002326:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
018744,002327:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
018745,002328: 
018746,002329:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOESNT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW.
018747,002330:

018871,002454:                                                                                                  #  Page 440
018872,002455:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
018873,002456:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
018874,002457:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
018875,002458:                                                                                                  #  
018876,002459:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
018877,002460: 
018878,002461:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
018879,002462:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
018880,002463:                                                                                                  #        V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
018881,002464: 
018882,002465:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
018883,002466:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                             V27N01E(FCADR)E
018884,002467:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,     V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E     V27N01E(FCADR)E
018885,002468: 
018886,002469: 41,3353           34317        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
018887,002470: 41,3354           54777                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
018888,002471: 41,3355           31047                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
018889,002472: 41,3356           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
018890,002473: 41,3357           31017                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
018891,002474: 41,3360           04651                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
018892,002475: 41,3361           03363                           TC       DSPOCTWO                              
018893,002476: 41,3362           05155        ENDSPF             TC       ENDOFJOB

019264,002847:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT 2  TASK ADRES (12 BIT)

019271,002854:

019273,002856:                                                                                                  #  TC ENDOFJOB INTO MPAC+3.  IT WILL TAKE TIME DELAY OUT OF MPAC+4 AND
019274,002857:                                                                                                  #  LEAVE IT IN A, INHINT AND TC MPAC.
019275,002858:

019287,002870: 
019288,002871:                                                                                                  #  Page 449
019289,002872:                                                                                                  #  PROCKEY PERFORMS THE SAME FUNCTION AS VBPROC. IT MUST BE CALLED UNDER
019290,002873:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CONTROL, WITH CHRPRIO.
019291,002874:

019293,002876: 40,3453           55013                           TS       REQRET
