019297,002880: 
019298,002881:                                                                                                  #  VBRESEQ WAKES ENDIDLE AT SAME LINE AS FINAL ENTER OF LOAD (L+3).
019299,002882:                                                                                                  #  (MAIN USE IS INTENDED AS RESPONSE TO INTERNALLY INITIATED FLASHING
019300,002883:                                                                                                  #   DISPLAYS IN ENDIDLE. SHOULD NOT BE USED WITH LOAD VERBS, PLEASE PERFORM,
019301,002884:                                                                                                  #   OR PLEASE MARK VERBS BECAUSE THEY ALREADY USE L+3 IN ANOTHER CONTEXT.)
019302,002885: 
019303,002886: 40,3457           44755        VBRESEQ            CS       ZERO                                  #  MAKE IT LOOK LIKE DATA IN.
019304,002887: 40,3460           03443                           TC       VBPROC     +1                         
019305,002888: 
019306,002889:                                                                                                  #  FLASH IS TURNED OFF BY PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, REQUEQUENCE,
019307,002890:                                                                                                  #  END OF LOAD.
019308,002891: 
019309,002892:                                                                                                  #  Page 450
019310,002893: 
019311,002894:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
019312,002895: 
019313,002896:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
019314,002897: 
019315,002898:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
019316,002899:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
019317,002900:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
019318,002901:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
019319,002902: 
019320,002903:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
019321,002904:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
019322,002905:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
019323,002906: 
019324,002907:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
019325,002908:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
019326,002909:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
019327,002910:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
019328,002911:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
019329,002912:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
019330,002913:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEYRLSE WILL
019331,002914:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEOFRE HE OBSCURED
019332,002915:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST. THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
019333,002916:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
019334,002917:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
019335,002918: 
019336,002919: 40,3461           44751        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
019337,002920: 40,3462           00006                           EXTEND                                         
019338,002921: 40,3463           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
019339,002922: 40,3464           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
019340,002923: 40,3465           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019341,002924: 40,3466           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
019342,002925: 40,3467           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019343,002926: 40,3470           03477                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
019344,002927: 40,3471           04457        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
019345,002928: 40,3472           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
019346,002929: 40,3473           03475                           TC       +2                                    #        DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
019347,002930: 40,3474           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019348,002931: 40,3475           04635                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
019349,002932: 40,3476           21050                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
019350,002933: 40,3477           34755        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
019351,002934: 40,3500           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #        JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
019352,002935: 40,3501           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
019353,002936: 40,3502           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #        CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
019354,002937: 40,3503           04502                           TC       RELDSP1                               
019355,002938: 40,3504           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019356,002939: 
019357,002940: 40,3505                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
019358,002941: 
019359,002942:                                                                                                  #  Page 451
019360,002943:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUBROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
019361,002944:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
019362,002945:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
019363,002946:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
019364,002947:                                                                                                  #  V'S ARE THE 7-BIT VERB CODE.  N'S ARE THE 7-BIT NOUN CODE.
019365,002948: 
019366,002949:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WTIH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
019367,002950:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS -
019368,002951:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R'S ONLY.
019369,002952: 
019370,002953:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WTIH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
019371,002954:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
019372,002955: 
019373,002956:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019374,002957:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAIALBLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
019375,002958:                                                                                                  #  IF V'S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
019376,002959:                                                                                                  #  ACTION). IF N'S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO
019377,002960:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
019378,002961: 
019379,002962:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019380,002963:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
019381,002964:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
019382,002965:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
019383,002966: 
019384,002967:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
019385,002968:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET.
019386,002969:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
019387,002970:                                                                                                  #  PROCED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
019388,002971:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
019389,002972:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
019390,002973:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
019391,002974: 
019392,002975:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
019393,002976:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AND EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR).
019394,002977: 
019395,002978:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
019396,002979:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
019397,002980: 
019398,002981:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
019399,002982:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
019400,002983: 
019401,002984:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR 'PLEASE PERFORM' SITUATIONS
019402,002985:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK).  FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
019403,002986:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THE REGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
019404,002987:                                                                                                  #  'CHECKLIST' NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE 'CHECKLIST'
019405,002988:                                                                                                  #  NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WTIH THE 'PLEASE PERFORM' VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
019406,002989:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS 'PASTES UP' THE 'PLEASE PERFORM' VERB INTO THE VERB
019407,002990:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
019408,002991: 
019409,002992:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL
019410,002993:                                                                                                  #  Page 452
019411,002994:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L. IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
019412,002995:                                                                                                  #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASED INT THE VERB
019413,002996:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
019414,002997:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
019415,002998:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
019416,002999:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.)  IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
019417,003000:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
019418,003001:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB.  IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
019419,003002:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
019420,003003: 
019421,003004:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
019422,003005:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
019423,003006: 
019424,003007:    4154                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1                         
019425,003008: 
019426,003009:    4154                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019427,003010:    4154           22007        NVSUB              LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019428,003011:    4155           54123        NVMONOPT           TS       NVTEMP                                
019429,003012:    4156           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019430,003013:    4157           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
019431,003014:    4160           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
019432,003015:    4161           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019433,003016:    4162           00002                           TC       Q                                     #  DSP SYST BLOCKED, RET TO 1+ CALLING LOC
019434,003017:    4163           34753                           CAF      ONE                                   #  DSP SYST AVAILABLE.
019435,003018:    4164           60002        NVSBCOM            AD       Q                                     
019436,003019:    4165           55037                           TS       NVQTEM                                #  2+ CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM
019437,003020:    4166           23022                           LXCH     MONSAVE2                              #  STORE NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019438,003021:    4167           04204                           TC       KILMONON                              #  TURN ON KILL MONITOR BIT
019439,003022:    4170           34201        NVSUBCOM           CAF      NVSBBBNK                              
019440,003023: 
019441,003024:    4171           56006                           XCH      BBANK                                 
019442,003025:    4172           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  SAVE OLD SUPERBITS
019443,003026:    4173           04007                           ROR      SUPERBNK                              
019444,003027:    4174           55040                           TS       NVBNKTEM

019446,003029:    4176           00006                           EXTEND

019449,003032:    4201     0777                                  EBANK=   DSPCOUNT                              
019450,003033:    4201           62101        NVSBBBNK           BBCON    NVSUB1                                
019451,003034: 
019452,003035:    4202     4201               PINSUPBT           =        NVSBBBNK                              #  CONTAINS THE PINBALL SUPERBITS.
019453,003036: 
019454,003037:    4202           53040        NVSUBEND           DXCH     NVQTEM                                #  NVBNKTEM MUST = NVQTEM+1
019455,003038:    4203           05165                           TC       SUPDXCHZ                              #  DTCB WITH SUPERBIT SWITCHING
019456,003039: 
019457,003040: 41,3516                                           SETLOC   ENDRQWT    +1                         
019458,003041: 
019459,003042: 41,3516                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019460,003043: 
019461,003044:                                                                                                  #  BLANKDSP BLANKS DISPLAY ACCORDING TO OPTION NUMBER IN NVTEMP AS FOLLOWS
019462,003045:                                                                                                  #  Page 453
019463,003046:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R'S ONLY.
019464,003047: 
019465,003048: 41,3516           64757        BLANKDSP           AD       SEVEN                                 #  7,8,9, OR 10 (A HAD 0,1,2,OR 3)
019466,003049: 41,3517           00004                           INHINT

019502,003085:                                                                                                  #                USES MPAC, +1, +2).

019504,003087: 41,3563           03571                           TC       NVSUB2                                #  IF NOUN NOT +0, GO ON
019505,003088: 41,3564           30160                           CA       MPAC       +4

019507,003090: 41,3566           34755                           CAF      ZERO                                  #  XERO REQRET SO THAT PASTED VERBS CAN
019508,003091: 41,3567           55013                           TS       REQRET                                #  BE EXECUTED BY OPERATOR.
019509,003092: 41,3570           04202        ENTSET             TC       NVSUBEND                              
019510,003093: 41,3571           10160        NVSUB2             CCS      MPAC       +4                         #  TEST VERB
019511,003094: 41,3572           03576                           TC       +4                                    #  IF VERB NOT +0, GO ON
019512,003095: 41,3573           30157                           CA       MPAC       +3                         
019513,003096:                                                                                                  #  Page 454
019514,003097: 41,3574           02317                           TC       UPDATNN    -1                         #  IF VERB = +0, DISPLAY NOUN, THEN RETURN
019515,003098: 41,3575           04202                           TC       NVSUBEND                              
019516,003099: 41,3576           30156                           CA       MPAC       +2                         #  TEMP FOR MACH CADR TO BE SPEC. (DSPDECVN
019517,003100: 41,3577           54161                           TS       MPAC       +5                         #        USES MPAC, +1, +2)
019518,003101: 41,3600           30160                           CA       MPAC       +4

019520,003103: 41,3602           30157                           CA       MPAC       +3                         #  BOTH AND GO TO ENTPAS0.
019521,003104: 41,3603           02317                           TC       UPDATNN    -1                         
019522,003105: 41,3604           34755                           CAF      ZERO

019524,003107: 41,3606           55015                           TS       CLPASS

019526,003109: 41,3610           30161                           CA       MPAC       +5                         #  RESTORES MACH CADR TO BE SPEC TO MPAC+2
019527,003110: 41,3611           54156                           TS       MPAC       +2                         #  FOR USE IN INTMCTBS (IN ENTPAS0).
019528,003111: 41,3612           02035        ENDNVSB1           TC       ENTPAS0                               
019529,003112: 
019530,003113:                                                                                                  #  IF INTERNAL MACH CADR TO BE SPECIFIED, MPAC+2 WILL BE PLACED INTO
019531,003114:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN ENTPAS0 (INTMCTBS).
019532,003115: 
019533,003116:    4204                                           SETLOC   NVSUBEND   +2                         
019534,003117:    4204                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019535,003118:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
019536,003119:    4204           34735        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #        THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
019537,003120:    4205           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
019538,003121:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR BIT.
019539,003122:    4206           00002                           TC       Q                                     
019540,003123: 
019541,003124:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      +0      INACTIVE (WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
019542,003125:                                                                                                  #                +1      PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019543,003126:                                                                                                  #                -1      TERMINATE. SET BY SPECIAL VERB.
019544,003127:                                                                                                  #                -0              DATA IN         SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
019545,003128:                                                                                                  #                        OR      RESEQUENCE      SET BY VERB 32
019546,003129: 
019547,003130:                                                                                                  #  L TO ENDIDLE (FIXED FIXED)
019548,003131:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
019549,003132:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
019550,003133:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019551,003134:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019552,003135:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
019553,003136:                                                                                                  #        L+1     FOR TERMINATE
019554,003137:                                                                                                  #        L+2     FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
019555,003138:                                                                                                  #        L+3     FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
019556,003139:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DTA.
019557,003140: 
019558,003141:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 1206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP
019559,003142:                                                                                                  #  Page 455
019560,003143:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
019561,003144:                                                                                                  #  1)    CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
019562,003145:                                                                                                  #        EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDDLE.)
019563,003146:                                                                                                  #  2)    DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
019564,003147:                                                                                                  #        NVSUBUSY.
019565,003148: 
019566,003149:    4207           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
019567,003150:    4210           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
019568,003151:    4211           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
019569,003152:    4212           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOC TO 1 SO CAN USE
019570,003153:    4213           75012                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
019571,003154:    4214           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
019572,003155:    4215           55042                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
019573,003156:    4216           05133                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019574,003157: 
019575,003158:    4217           05155        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019576,003159: 
019577,003160:    4220           11042        ISCADR+0           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019578,003161:    4221           04227                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.
019579,003162:    4222           00002                           TC       Q                                     
019580,003163:    4223           04227                           TC       DSPABORT

019583,003166:    4225           04227                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF DSPLIST = +0.
019584,003167:    4226           00002                           TC       Q                                     
019585,003168:    4227           05652        DSPABORT           TC       P00DOO                                
019586,003169:    4230           01206                           OCT      01206

019618,003201: 
019619,003202:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB BLANKS ANY COMBINATION OF R1, R2, R3.
019620,003203:                                                                                                  #  CALL WITH BLANKING CODE IN A.
019621,003204:                                                                                                  #  BIT1=1 BLANKS R1, BIT2=1 BLANKS R2, BIT3=1 BLANKS R3.
019622,003205:                                                                                                  #  ANY COMBINATION OF THESE BITS IS ACCEPTED.
019623,003206:

019880,003463:                                                                                                  #   WHEN THEY CONTAIN THE SF CONSTANTS.)
019881,003464:

019883,003466:    4416           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019884,003467:    4417           30135                           CA       MPTEMP                                #  C(A) +, DO REGULAR SHORTMP
019885,003468:    4420           17310                           TCF      SHORTMP    +1                         #  C(A) +0, DO REGULAR SHORTMP
019886,003469:    4421           14417                           TCF      -2                                    #  C(A) -, DO REGULAR SHORTMP

019902,003485: 
019903,003486:                                                                                                  #  Page 463
019904,003487:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM.
019905,003488: 
019906,003489:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
019907,003490:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
019908,003491:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
019909,003492:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
019910,003493: 
019911,003494:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019912,003495:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1) BY ENDIDLE
019913,003496:                                                                                                  #                2) BY NVSUBUSY
019914,003497:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
019915,003498:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019916,003499:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
019917,003500:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
019918,003501: 
019919,003502:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
019920,003503:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
019921,003504:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
019922,003505:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
019923,003506:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
019924,003507: 
019925,003508:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
019926,003509:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019927,003510:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
019928,003511:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019929,003512:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019930,003513: 
019931,003514:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
019932,003515:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
019933,003516:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
019934,003517: 
019935,003518: 
019936,003519:                                                                                                  #  .
019937,003520: 
019938,003521:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
019939,003522:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
019940,003523:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
019941,003524:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
019942,003525: 
019943,003526:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019944,003527:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
019945,003528:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
019946,003529:                                                                                                  #  1)    DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
019947,003530:                                                                                                  #        IS EXCEEDED.
019948,003531:                                                                                                  #  2)    CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING
019949,003532:                                                                                                  #  Page 464
019950,003533:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019951,003534: 
019952,003535:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
019953,003536:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
019954,003537:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
019955,003538:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
019956,003539:    4443           10647                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
019957,003540:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
019958,003541: 
019959,003542:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
019960,003543:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
019961,003544: 
019962,003545: 04,2647                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
019963,003546: 04,2647                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019964,003547: 04,2647           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
019965,003548: 04,2650           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019966,003549: 04,2651           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
019967,003550: 04,2652           04374                           TC       RELDSPON                              
019968,003551: 04,2653           30001                           CA       L                                     
019969,003552: 04,2654           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
019970,003553: 04,2655           05133        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019971,003554: 
019972,003555:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
019973,003556:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
019974,003557:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
019975,003558:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
019976,003559:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
019977,003560: 
019978,003561:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
019979,003562:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019980,003563:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019981,003564:    4446           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
019982,003565:    4447           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019983,003566:    4450           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
019984,003567:    4451           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
019985,003568:    4452           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019986,003569:    4453           14455                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
019987,003570:    4454           14164                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
019988,003571:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
019989,003572:    4455           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2. PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
019990,003573:    4456           14437                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
019991,003574: 
019992,003575:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
019993,003576:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
019994,003577:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.

020139,003722:                                                                                                  #  Page 470
020140,003723:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF:
020141,003724:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
020142,003725:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
020143,003726:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
020144,003727:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROS THE 'TEST ALARM' OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY, RESTART.
020145,003728:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS 'CAUTION RESET' TO 1.
020146,003729:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
